## <a name="locked-deployment-files"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-823">Arquivos de implantação bloqueados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-823">Locked deployment files</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-824">Os arquivos na pasta de implantação são bloqueados quando o aplicativo está em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-824">Files in the deployment folder are locked when the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-825">Os arquivos bloqueados não podem ser substituídos durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-825">Locked files can't be overwritten during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-826">Para liberar os arquivos bloqueados em uma implantação, interrompa o pool de aplicativos usando **uma** das abordagens a seguir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-826">To release locked files in a deployment, stop the app pool using **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-827">Use a Implantação da Web e referencie `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` no arquivo do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-827">Use Web Deploy and reference `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` in the project file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-828">Um arquivo *app_offline.htm* é colocado na raiz do diretório de aplicativo da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-828">An *app_offline.htm* file is placed at the root of the web app directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-829">Quando o arquivo estiver presente, o módulo do ASP.NET Core apenas desligará o aplicativo e servirá o arquivo *app_offline.htm* durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-829">When the file is present, the ASP.NET Core Module gracefully shuts down the app and serves the *app_offline.htm* file during the deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-830">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Referência de configuração do módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-830">For more information, see the [ASP.NET Core Module configuration reference](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-831">Manualmente interrompa o pool de aplicativos no Gerenciador do IIS no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-831">Manually stop the app pool in the IIS Manager on the server.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-832">Use o PowerShell para descartar *app_offline.htm* (requer o PowerShell 5 ou posterior):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-832">Use PowerShell to drop *app_offline.htm* (requires PowerShell 5 or later):</span></span>

  ```powershell
  $pathToApp = 'PATH_TO_APP'

  # Stop the AppPool
  New-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  # Provide script commands here to deploy the app

  # Restart the AppPool
  Remove-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  ```

## <a name="data-protection"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-833">Proteção de dados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-833">Data protection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-834">A [pilha Proteção de Dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) é usada por vários [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) ASP.NET Core, incluindo aqueles usados na autenticação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-834">The [ASP.NET Core Data Protection stack](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) is used by several ASP.NET Core [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index), including middleware used in authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-835">Mesmo se as APIs de proteção de dados não forem chamadas pelo código do usuário, a proteção de dados deverá ser configurada com um script de implantação ou no código do usuário para criar um [repositório de chaves](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management) criptográfico persistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-835">Even if Data Protection APIs aren't called by user code, data protection should be configured with a deployment script or in user code to create a persistent cryptographic [key store](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-836">Se a proteção de dados não estiver configurada, as chaves serão mantidas na memória e descartadas quando o aplicativo for reiniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-836">If data protection isn't configured, the keys are held in memory and discarded when the app restarts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-837">Se o token de autenticação for armazenado na memória quando o aplicativo for reiniciado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-837">If the key ring is stored in memory when the app restarts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-838">Os cookie tokens de autenticação baseados em todos os são invalidados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-838">All cookie-based authentication tokens are invalidated.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-839">Os usuários precisam entrar novamente na próxima solicitação deles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-839">Users are required to sign in again on their next request.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-840">Todos os dados protegidos com o token de autenticação não poderão mais ser descriptografados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-840">Any data protected with the key ring can no longer be decrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-841">Isso pode incluir [tokens CSRF](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) e [ASP.NET Core cookie s de TempData do MVC](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-841">This may include [CSRF tokens](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) and [ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookies](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-842">Para configurar a proteção de dados no IIS para persistir o token de autenticação, use **uma** das seguintes abordagens:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-842">To configure data protection under IIS to persist the key ring, use **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-843">**Criar chaves de registro de proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-843">**Create Data Protection Registry Keys**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-844">As chaves de proteção de dados usadas pelos aplicativos ASP.NET Core são armazenadas no registro externo aos aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-844">Data protection keys used by ASP.NET Core apps are stored in the registry external to the apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-845">Para persistir as chaves de determinado aplicativo, crie uma chave de registro para o pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-845">To persist the keys for a given app, create registry keys for the app pool.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-846">Para instalações autônomas do IIS não Web Farm, você pode usar o [script Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 de Proteção de Dados do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) para cada pool de aplicativos usado com um aplicativo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-846">For standalone, non-webfarm IIS installations, the [Data Protection Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) can be used for each app pool used with an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-847">Esse script cria uma chave de registro no registro HKLM que é acessível apenas para a conta do processo de trabalho do pool de aplicativos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-847">This script creates a registry key in the HKLM registry that's accessible only to the worker process account of the app's app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-848">As chaves são criptografadas em repouso usando a DPAPI com uma chave para todo o computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-848">Keys are encrypted at rest using DPAPI with a machine-wide key.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-849">Em cenários de web farm, um aplicativo pode ser configurado para usar um caminho UNC para armazenar seu token de autenticação de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-849">In web farm scenarios, an app can be configured to use a UNC path to store its data protection key ring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-850">Por padrão, as chaves de proteção de dados não são criptografadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-850">By default, the data protection keys aren't encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-851">Garanta que as permissões de arquivo de o compartilhamento de rede sejam limitadas à conta do Windows na qual o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-851">Ensure that the file permissions for the network share are limited to the Windows account the app runs under.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-852">Um certificado X509 pode ser usado para proteger chaves em repouso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-852">An X509 certificate can be used to protect keys at rest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-853">Considere um mecanismo para permitir aos usuários carregar certificados: coloque os certificados no repositório de certificados confiáveis do usuário e certifique-se de que eles estejam disponíveis em todos os computadores nos quais o aplicativo do usuário é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-853">Consider a mechanism to allow users to upload certificates: Place certificates into the user's trusted certificate store and ensure they're available on all machines where the user's app runs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-854">Veja [Configurar a proteção de dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) para obter detalhes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-854">See [Configure ASP.NET Core Data Protection](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) for details.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-855">**Configurar o pool de aplicativos do IIS para carregar o perfil do usuário**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-855">**Configure the IIS Application Pool to load the user profile**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-856">Essa configuração está na seção **Modelo de processo** nas **Configurações avançadas** do pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-856">This setting is in the **Process Model** section under the **Advanced Settings** for the app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-857">Defina **carregar perfil do usuário** como `True` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-857">Set **Load User Profile** to `True`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-858">Quando definido como `True`, as chaves são armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário e protegidas usando DPAPI com uma chave específica para a conta de usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-858">When set to `True`, keys are stored in the user profile directory and protected using DPAPI with a key specific to the user account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-859">As chaves são persistidas para a pasta *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-859">Keys are persisted to the *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys* folder.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-860">O [atributo setProfileEnvironment](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) do pool de aplicativos também deve ser habilitado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-860">The app pool's [setProfileEnvironment attribute](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) must also be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-861">O valor padrão de `setProfileEnvironment` é `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-861">The default value of `setProfileEnvironment` is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-862">Em alguns cenários (por exemplo, um SO Windows), `setProfileEnvironment` é definido como `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-862">In some scenarios (for example, Windows OS), `setProfileEnvironment` is set to `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-863">Se as chaves não estiverem armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário como esperado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-863">If keys aren't stored in the user profile directory as expected:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-864">navegue até a pasta *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-864">Navigate to the *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config* folder.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-865">Abra o arquivo *applicationHost.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-865">Open the *applicationHost.config* file.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-866">Localize o elemento `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-866">Locate the `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` element.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-867">Confirme se o atributo `setProfileEnvironment` não está presente, que tem como padrão o valor `true`, ou defina explicitamente o valor do atributo como `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-867">Confirm that the `setProfileEnvironment` attribute isn't present, which defaults the value to `true`, or explicitly set the attribute's value to `true`.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-868">**Usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-868">**Use the file system as a key ring store**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-869">Ajuste o código do aplicativo para [usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-869">Adjust the app code to [use the file system as a key ring store](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-870">Use um certificado X509 para proteger o token de autenticação e verifique se ele é um certificado confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-870">Use an X509 certificate to protect the key ring and ensure the certificate is a trusted certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-871">Se o certificado for autoassinado, você deverá colocá-lo no repositório Raiz confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-871">If the certificate is self-signed, place the certificate in the Trusted Root store.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-872">Ao usar o IIS em uma web farm:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-872">When using IIS in a web farm:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-873">Use um compartilhamento de arquivos que pode ser acessado por todos os computadores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-873">Use a file share that all machines can access.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-874">Implante um certificado X509 em cada computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-874">Deploy an X509 certificate to each machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-875">Configure a [proteção de dados no código](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-875">Configure [data protection in code](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-876">**Definir uma política para todo o computador para proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-876">**Set a machine-wide policy for data protection**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-877">O sistema de proteção de dados tem suporte limitado para a configuração da [política de todo o computador](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) padrão para todos os aplicativos que consomem as APIs de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-877">The data protection system has limited support for setting a default [machine-wide policy](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) for all apps that consume the Data Protection APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-878">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-878">For more information, see <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span></span>

## <a name="virtual-directories"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-879">Diretórios virtuais</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-879">Virtual Directories</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-880">[Diretórios virtuais IIS](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) não são compatíveis com aplicativos ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-880">[IIS Virtual Directories](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) aren't supported with ASP.NET Core apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-881">Um aplicativo pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo](#sub-applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-881">An app can be hosted as a [sub-application](#sub-applications).</span></span>

## <a name="sub-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-882">Subaplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-882">Sub-applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-883">Um aplicativo ASP.NET Core pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo IIS (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-883">An ASP.NET Core app can be hosted as an [IIS sub-application (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-884">A parte do caminho do subaplicativo se torna parte da URL raiz do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-884">The sub-app's path becomes part of the root app's URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-885">Links de ativos estáticos dentro do subaplicativo devem usar a notação de sinal de til e barra (`~/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-885">Static asset links within the sub-app should use tilde-slash (`~/`) notation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-886">A notação de sinal de til e barra aciona um [Auxiliar de Marca](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) para preceder a base de caminho do subaplicativo ao link relativo renderizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-886">Tilde-slash notation triggers a [Tag Helper](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) to prepend the sub-app's pathbase to the rendered relative link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-887">Para um subaplicativo no `/subapp_path`, uma imagem vinculada com `src="~/image.png"` é renderizada como `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-887">For a sub-app at `/subapp_path`, an image linked with `src="~/image.png"` is rendered as `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-888">O Middleware de Arquivo Estático do aplicativo raiz não processa a solicitação de arquivo estático.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-888">The root app's Static File Middleware doesn't process the static file request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-889">A solicitação é processada pelo Middleware de Arquivo Estático do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-889">The request is processed by the sub-app's Static File Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-890">Se um atributo de ativo estático `src` for definido como um caminho absoluto (por exemplo, `src="/image.png"`), o link será renderizado sem a base de caminho do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-890">If a static asset's `src` attribute is set to an absolute path (for example, `src="/image.png"`), the link is rendered without the sub-app's pathbase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-891">O Middleware de Arquivos Estáticos do aplicativo raiz tenta fornecer o ativo do [webroot](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root) da raiz do aplicativo, que resulta em uma resposta *404 – Não encontrado*, a menos que o ativo estático esteja disponível no aplicativo raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-891">The root app's Static File Middleware attempts to serve the asset from the root app's [web root](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root), which results in a *404 - Not Found* response unless the static asset is available from the root app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-892">Para hospedar um aplicativo ASP.NET Core como um subaplicativo em outro aplicativo do ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-892">To host an ASP.NET Core app as a sub-app under another ASP.NET Core app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-893">Estabeleça um pool de aplicativos para o subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-893">Establish an app pool for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-894">Defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** porque o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) do .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho, não no CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-894">Set the **.NET CLR Version** to **No Managed Code** because the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process, not the desktop CLR (.NET CLR).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-895">Adicione o site raiz no Gerenciador do IIS com o subaplicativo em uma pasta no site raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-895">Add the root site in IIS Manager with the sub-app in a folder under the root site.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-896">Clique com o botão direito do mouse na pasta do subaplicativo no Gerenciador do IIS e selecione **Converter em aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-896">Right-click the sub-app folder in IIS Manager and select **Convert to Application**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-897">Na caixa de diálogo **Adicionar Aplicativo**, use o botão **Selecionar** no **Pool de Aplicativos** para atribuir o pool de aplicativos que você criou ao subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-897">In the **Add Application** dialog, use the **Select** button for the **Application Pool** to assign the app pool that you created for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-898">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-898">Select **OK**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-899">A atribuição de um pool de aplicativos separado para o subaplicativo é um requisito ao usar o modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-899">The assignment of a separate app pool to the sub-app is a requirement when using the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-900">Para obter mais informações sobre o modelo de hospedagem em processo e como configurar o módulo ASP.NET Core, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-900">For more information on the in-process hosting model and configuring the ASP.NET Core Module, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-of-iis-with-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-901">Configuração do IIS com web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-901">Configuration of IIS with web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-902">A configuração do IIS é influenciada pela seção `<system.webServer>` do *web.config* para cenários do IIS que são funcionais para aplicativos ASP.NET Core com o Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-902">IIS configuration is influenced by the `<system.webServer>` section of *web.config* for IIS scenarios that are functional for ASP.NET Core apps with the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-903">Por exemplo, a configuração do IIS é funcional para a compactação dinâmica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-903">For example, IIS configuration is functional for dynamic compression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-904">Se o IIS for configurado no nível do servidor para usar a compactação dinâmica, o elemento `<urlCompression>` no arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo pode desabilitá-la para um aplicativo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-904">If IIS is configured at the server level to use dynamic compression, the `<urlCompression>` element in the app's *web.config* file can disable it for an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-905">Para obter mais informações, consulte estes tópicos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-905">For more information, see the following topics:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-906">Referência de configuração para\<system.webServer></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-906">Configuration reference for \<system.webServer></span></span>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/)
* <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>
* <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-907">Para definir variáveis de ambiente para aplicativos individuais em execução em pools de aplicativos isolados (com suporte para o IIS 10,0 ou posterior), consulte a seção de *AppCmd.exe comando* do tópico [variáveis \<environmentVariables> de ambiente](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) na documentação de referência do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-907">To set environment variables for individual apps running in isolated app pools (supported for IIS 10.0 or later), see the *AppCmd.exe command* section of the [Environment Variables \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) topic in the IIS reference documentation.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-sections-of-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-908">Seções de configuração de web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-908">Configuration sections of web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-909">As seções de configuração de aplicativos ASP.NET 4.x em *web.config* não são usadas por aplicativos ASP.NET Core para configuração:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-909">Configuration sections of ASP.NET 4.x apps in *web.config* aren't used by ASP.NET Core apps for configuration:</span></span>

* `<system.web>`
* `<appSettings>`
* `<connectionStrings>`
* `<location>`

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-910">Aplicativos ASP.NET Core são configurados para usar outros provedores de configuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-910">ASP.NET Core apps are configured using other configuration providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-911">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-911">For more information, see [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span></span>

## <a name="application-pools"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-912">Pools de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-912">Application Pools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-913">O isolamento do pool de aplicativos é determinado pelo modelo de hospedagem:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-913">App pool isolation is determined by the hosting model:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-914">Hospedagem em processo: os aplicativos devem ser executados em pools de aplicativos separados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-914">In-process hosting: Apps are required to run in separate app pools.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-915">Hospedagem fora do processo: é recomendável isolar os aplicativos uns dos outros executando cada aplicativo em seu próprio pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-915">Out-of-process hosting: We recommend isolating the apps from each other by running each app in its own app pool.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-916">A caixa de diálogo **Adicionar Site** do IIS usa como padrão um único pool de aplicativos por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-916">The IIS **Add Website** dialog defaults to a single app pool per app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-917">Quando um **Nome de site** é fornecido, o texto é transferido automaticamente para a caixa de texto **Pool de aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-917">When a **Site name** is provided, the text is automatically transferred to the **Application pool** textbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-918">Um novo pool de aplicativos é criado usando o nome do site quando você adicionar o site.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-918">A new app pool is created using the site name when the site is added.</span></span>

## <a name="application-pool-no-locidentity"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-919">Pool de aplicativosIdentity</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-919">Application Pool Identity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-920">Uma conta de identidade do pool de aplicativos permite executar um aplicativo em uma conta exclusiva sem a necessidade de criar e gerenciar domínios ou contas locais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-920">An app pool identity account allows an app to run under a unique account without having to create and manage domains or local accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-921">No IIS 8.0 ou posterior, o WAS (Processo de trabalho do administrador) do IIS cria uma conta virtual com o nome do novo pool de aplicativos e executa os processos de trabalho do pool de aplicativos nesta conta por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-921">On IIS 8.0 or later, the IIS Admin Worker Process (WAS) creates a virtual account with the name of the new app pool and runs the app pool's worker processes under this account by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-922">No console de gerenciamento do IIS, em **Configurações avançadas** para o pool de aplicativos, verifique se o **Identity** está definido para usar \*\*ApplicationPool Identity \*\*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-922">In the IIS Management Console under **Advanced Settings** for the app pool, ensure that the **Identity** is set to use **ApplicationPoolIdentity**:</span></span>

![Caixa de diálogo Configurações avançadas do pool de aplicativos](index/_static/apppool-identity.png)

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-924">O processo de gerenciamento do IIS cria um identificador seguro com o nome do pool de aplicativos no Sistema de segurança do Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-924">The IIS management process creates a secure identifier with the name of the app pool in the Windows Security System.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-925">Os recursos podem ser protegidos usando essa identidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-925">Resources can be secured using this identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-926">No entanto, essa identidade não é uma conta de usuário real e não será mostrada no Console de Gerenciamento de Usuários do Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-926">However, this identity isn't a real user account and doesn't show up in the Windows User Management Console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-927">Se o processo de trabalho do IIS requerer acesso elevado ao aplicativo, modifique a ACL (lista de controle de acesso) do diretório que contém o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-927">If the IIS worker process requires elevated access to the app, modify the Access Control List (ACL) for the directory containing the app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-928">Abra o Windows Explorer e navegue para o diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-928">Open Windows Explorer and navigate to the directory.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-929">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no diretório e selecione **Propriedades**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-929">Right-click on the directory and select **Properties**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-930">Na guia **Segurança**, selecione o botão **Editar** e, em seguida, no botão **Adicionar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-930">Under the **Security** tab, select the **Edit** button and then the **Add** button.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-931">Clique no botão **Locais** e verifique se o sistema está selecionado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-931">Select the **Locations** button and make sure the system is selected.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-932">Insira **IIS AppPool\\<nome_pool_aplicativos>** na área **Inserir os nomes de objeto a serem selecionados**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-932">Enter **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** in **Enter the object names to select** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-933">Selecione o botão **Verificar Nomes**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-933">Select the **Check Names** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-934">Para o *DefaultAppPool*, verifique os nomes usando **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-934">For the *DefaultAppPool* check the names using **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-935">Quando o botão **Verificar Nomes** é selecionado, um valor de **DefaultAppPool** é indicado na área de nomes de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-935">When the **Check Names** button is selected, a value of **DefaultAppPool** is indicated in the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-936">Não é possível inserir o nome do pool de aplicativos diretamente na área de nomes de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-936">It isn't possible to enter the app pool name directly into the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-937">Use o formato **IIS AppPool\\<nome_pool_aplicativos>** ao verificar o nome do objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-937">Use the **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** format when checking for the object name.</span></span>

   ![Selecione a caixa de diálogo de usuários ou grupos para a pasta do aplicativo: o nome do pool de aplicativos "DefaultAppPool" é anexado ao "IIS AppPool\" na área de nomes de objeto antes de selecionar"Verificar Nomes".](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-1.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-939">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-939">Select **OK**.</span></span>

   ![Selecione a caixa de diálogo de usuários ou grupos para a pasta do aplicativo: depois de selecionar "Verificar Nomes", o nome do objeto "DefaultAppPool" é mostrado na área de nomes de objeto.](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-2.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-941">As permissões de leitura &amp; execução devem ser concedidas por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-941">Read &amp; execute permissions should be granted by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-942">Forneça permissões adicionais conforme necessário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-942">Provide additional permissions as needed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-943">O acesso também pode ser concedido por meio de um prompt de comando usando a ferramenta **ICACLS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-943">Access can also be granted at a command prompt using the **ICACLS** tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-944">Usando o *DefaultAppPool* como exemplo, o comando a seguir é usado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-944">Using the *DefaultAppPool* as an example, the following command is used:</span></span>

```console
ICACLS C:\sites\MyWebApp /grant "IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool":F
```

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-945">Para saber mais, veja o tópico [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-945">For more information, see the [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) topic.</span></span>

## <a name="http2-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-946">Suporte do HTTP/2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-946">HTTP/2 support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-947">O [HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) é compatível com ASP.NET Core nos seguintes cenários de implantação de IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-947">[HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) is supported with ASP.NET Core in the following IIS deployment scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-948">Em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-948">In-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-949">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 ou posterior; IIS 10 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-949">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-950">Conexão TLS 1.2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-950">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-951">Fora do processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-951">Out-of-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-952">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 ou posterior; IIS 10 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-952">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-953">Conexões de servidor de borda voltadas para o público usam HTTP/2, mas a conexão de proxy reverso para o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) usa HTTP/1.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-953">Public-facing edge server connections use HTTP/2, but the reverse proxy connection to the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) uses HTTP/1.1.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-954">Conexão TLS 1.2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-954">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-955">Para uma implantação em processo quando uma conexão HTTP/2 for estabelecida, o [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) relatará `HTTP/2`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-955">For an in-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/2`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-956">Para uma implantação fora de processo quando uma conexão HTTP/2 for estabelecida, o [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) relatará `HTTP/1.1`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-956">For an out-of-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/1.1`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-957">Para saber mais sobre os modelos de hospedagem em processo e fora de processo, confira <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-957">For more information on the in-process and out-of-process hosting models, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-958">O HTTP/2 está habilitado por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-958">HTTP/2 is enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-959">As conexões retornarão para HTTP/1.1 se uma conexão HTTP/2 não for estabelecida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-959">Connections fall back to HTTP/1.1 if an HTTP/2 connection isn't established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-960">Para obter mais informações sobre a configuração de HTTP/2 com implantações do IIS, consulte [HTTP/2 no IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-960">For more information on HTTP/2 configuration with IIS deployments, see [HTTP/2 on IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span></span>

## <a name="cors-preflight-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-961">Solicitações de simulação do CORS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-961">CORS preflight requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-962">*Esta seção só se aplica a aplicativos ASP.NET Core com o .NET Framework como destino.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-962">*This section only applies to ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-963">Para um aplicativo ASP.NET Core com o .NET Framework como destino, as solicitações OPTIONS não são passadas para o aplicativo por padrão no IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-963">For an ASP.NET Core app that targets the .NET Framework, OPTIONS requests aren't passed to the app by default in IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-964">Para saber como configurar os manipuladores do IIS do aplicativo no *web.config* para passar solicitações de opções, consulte [habilitar solicitações entre origens no ASP.NET Web API 2: como o CORS funciona](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-964">To learn how to configure the app's IIS handlers in *web.config* to pass OPTIONS requests, see [Enable cross-origin requests in ASP.NET Web API 2: How CORS Works](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span></span>

## <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-965">Módulo de Inicialização de Aplicativo e Tempo Limite de Ociosidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-965">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-966">Quando hospedado no IIS pela versão 2 do Módulo do ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-966">When hosted in IIS by the ASP.NET Core Module version 2:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-967">[Módulo de inicialização do aplicativo](#application-initialization-module): hospedado [em processo](#in-process-hosting-model) ou [fora do processo](#out-of-process-hosting-model) do aplicativo pode ser configurado para iniciar automaticamente em uma reinicialização do processo de trabalho ou reinicialização do servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-967">[Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module): App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) or [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) can be configured to start automatically on a worker process restart or server restart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-968">[Tempo limite de ociosidade](#idle-timeout): o aplicativo hospedado [no processo](#in-process-hosting-model) pode ser configurado para não atingir o tempo limite durante períodos de inatividade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-968">[Idle Timeout](#idle-timeout): App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) can be configured not to timeout during periods of inactivity.</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-969">Módulo de Inicialização de Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-969">Application Initialization Module</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-970">*Aplica-se a aplicativos hospedados em processo e fora de processo.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-970">*Applies to apps hosted in-process and out-of-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-971">[Inicialização de Aplicativo IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization) é um recurso do IIS que envia uma solicitação HTTP para o aplicativo quando o pool de aplicativos é iniciado ou reciclado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-971">[IIS Application Initialization](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization) is an IIS feature that sends an HTTP request to the app when the app pool starts or is recycled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-972">A solicitação dispara a inicialização do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-972">The request triggers the app to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-973">Por padrão, o IIS emite uma solicitação para a URL raiz do aplicativo (`/`) para inicializar o aplicativo (confira mais detalhes sobre a configuração nos [recursos adicionais](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-973">By default, IIS issues a request to the app's root URL (`/`) to initialize the app (see the [additional resources](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources) for more details on configuration).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-974">Confirme se o recurso da função Inicialização de Aplicativo do IIS está habilitado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-974">Confirm that the IIS Application Initialization role feature in enabled:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-975">No Windows 7 ou sistemas de área de trabalho posteriores, ao usar o IIS localmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-975">On Windows 7 or later desktop systems when using IIS locally:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-976">Navegue até **Painel de Controle** > **Programas** > **Programas e Recursos** > **Ativar ou desativar recursos do Windows** (lado esquerdo da tela).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-976">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-977">Abra **Serviços de Informações da Internet** > **Serviços da World Wide Web** > **Recursos de Desenvolvimento de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-977">Open **Internet Information Services** > **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-978">Marque a caixa de seleção **Inicialização de Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-978">Select the check box for **Application Initialization**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-979">No Windows Server 2008 R2 ou posterior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-979">On Windows Server 2008 R2 or later:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-980">Abra o **Assistente de Adição de Funções e Recursos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-980">Open the **Add Roles and Features Wizard**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-981">No painel **Selecionar serviços de função**, abra o nó **Desenvolvimento de aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-981">In the **Select role services** panel, open the **Application Development** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-982">Marque a caixa de seleção **Inicialização de Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-982">Select the check box for **Application Initialization**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-983">Use quaisquer das abordagens a seguir para habilitar o Módulo de Inicialização do Aplicativo para o site:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-983">Use either of the following approaches to enable the Application Initialization Module for the site:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-984">Usando o Gerenciador do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-984">Using IIS Manager:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-985">Selecione **Pools de Aplicativos** no painel **Conexões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-985">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-986">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do aplicativo na lista e selecione **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-986">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-987">O **Modo de Inicialização** padrão é **OnDemand**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-987">The default **Start Mode** is **OnDemand**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-988">Defina o **Modo de Inicialização** como **AlwaysRunning**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-988">Set the **Start Mode** to **AlwaysRunning**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-989">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-989">Select **OK**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-990">Abra o nó **Sites** no painel **Conexões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-990">Open the **Sites** node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-991">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no aplicativo e selecione **Gerenciar Site** > **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-991">Right-click the app and select **Manage Website** > **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-992">A configuração de **Pré-carregamento Habilitado** padrão é **Falso**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-992">The default **Preload Enabled** setting is **False**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-993">Defina **Pré-carregamento Habilitado** como **Verdadeiro**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-993">Set **Preload Enabled** to **True**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-994">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-994">Select **OK**.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-995">Usando o *web.config*, adicione o elemento `<applicationInitialization>` definindo `doAppInitAfterRestart` como `true` aos elementos `<system.webServer>` no arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-995">Using *web.config*, add the `<applicationInitialization>` element with `doAppInitAfterRestart` set to `true` to the `<system.webServer>` elements in the app's *web.config* file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
  <configuration>
    <location path="." inheritInChildApplications="false">
      <system.webServer>
        <applicationInitialization doAppInitAfterRestart="true" />
      </system.webServer>
    </location>
  </configuration>
  ```

### <a name="idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-996">Tempo limite de ociosidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-996">Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-997">*Só se aplica a aplicativos hospedados em processo.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-997">*Only applies to apps hosted in-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-998">Para impedir que o aplicativo fique ocioso, defina o tempo limite de ociosidade do pool de aplicativos, usando o Gerenciador do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-998">To prevent the app from idling, set the app pool's idle timeout using IIS Manager:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-999">Selecione **Pools de Aplicativos** no painel **Conexões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-999">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1000">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do aplicativo na lista e selecione **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1000">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1001">O **Tempo Limite de Ociosidade (minutos)** é de **20** minutos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1001">The default **Idle Time-out (minutes)** is **20** minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1002">Defina o **Tempo Limite de Ociosidade (minutos)** como **0** (zero).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1002">Set the **Idle Time-out (minutes)** to **0** (zero).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1003">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1003">Select **OK**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1004">Recicle o processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1004">Recycle the worker process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1005">Para impedir que aplicativos hospedados [fora de processo](#out-of-process-hosting-model) atinjam o tempo limite, use uma das seguintes abordagens:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1005">To prevent apps hosted [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) from timing out, use either of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1006">Execute ping do aplicativo de um serviço externo para mantê-lo em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1006">Ping the app from an external service in order to keep it running.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1007">Se o aplicativo hospedar apenas serviços em segundo plano, evite a hospedagem do IIS e use um [Serviço do Windows para hospedar o aplicativo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1007">If the app only hosts background services, avoid IIS hosting and use a [Windows Service to host the ASP.NET Core app](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service).</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1008">Recursos adicionais do Módulo de Inicialização de Aplicativo e do Tempo Limite de Ociosidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1008">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout additional resources</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1011">[Configurações do modelo de processo para um \<processModel> pool de aplicativos ](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1011">[Process Model Settings for an Application Pool \<processModel>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel).</span></span>

## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1022">Sistemas operacionais compatíveis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1022">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1023">Há suporte para os seguintes sistemas operacionais:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1023">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1024">Windows 7 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1024">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1025">Windows Server 2008 R2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1025">Windows Server 2008 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1026">O [servidor HTTP.sys](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (anteriormente chamado de WebListener) não funciona em uma configuração de proxy reverso com o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1026">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1027">Use o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1027">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1028">Para obter mais informações sobre hospedagem no Azure, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1028">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1029">Para obter as diretrizes de solução de problemas, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1029">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1030">Plataformas com suporte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1030">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1031">Aplicativos publicados para implantação de 32 bits (x86) ou 64 bits (x64) têm suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1031">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1032">Implantar um aplicativo de 32 bits com um SDK do .NET Core de 32 bits (x86), a menos que o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1032">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1033">Exija o maior espaço de endereço de memória virtual disponível para um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1033">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1034">Exija o maior tamanho de pilha do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1034">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1035">Tenha dependências nativas de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1035">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1036">Use um SDK do .NET Core de 64 bits (x64) para publicar um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1036">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1037">Um runtime de 64 bits deve estar presente no sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1037">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1038">O ASP.NET Core vem com o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), um servidor HTTP padrão multiplataforma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1038">ASP.NET Core ships with [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), a default, cross-platform HTTP server.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1039">Ao usar o [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) ou o [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), o aplicativo é executado em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS (*fora do processo*) com o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1039">When using [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) or [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), the app runs in a process separate from the IIS worker process (*out-of-process*) with the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1040">Como os aplicativos ASP.NET Core são executados em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS, o módulo realiza o gerenciamento de processos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1040">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1041">O módulo inicia o processo para o aplicativo ASP.NET Core quando a primeira solicitação chega e reinicia o aplicativo se ele é desligado ou falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1041">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1042">Isso é basicamente o mesmo comportamento que o dos aplicativos que são executados dentro do processo e são gerenciados pelo [WAS (Serviço de Ativação de Processos do Windows)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1042">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1043">O diagrama a seguir ilustra a relação entre o IIS, o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e um aplicativo hospedado de fora d processo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1043">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![Módulo do ASP.NET Core](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1045">As solicitações chegam da Web para o driver do HTTP.sys no modo kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1045">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1046">O driver roteia as solicitações ao IIS na porta configurada do site, normalmente, a 80 (HTTP) ou a 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1046">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1047">O módulo encaminha as solicitações ao Kestrel em uma porta aleatória do aplicativo, que não seja a porta 80 ou 443.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1047">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1048">O módulo Especifica a porta por meio de uma variável de ambiente na inicialização, e o [middleware de integração do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configura o servidor a ser escutado `http://localhost:{port}` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1048">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the [IIS Integration Middleware](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{port}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1049">Outras verificações são executadas e as solicitações que não se originam do módulo são rejeitadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1049">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1050">O módulo não é compatível com encaminhamento de HTTPS, portanto, as solicitações são encaminhadas por HTTP, mesmo se recebidas pelo IIS por HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1050">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1051">Depois que o Kestrel coleta a solicitação do módulo, a solicitação é enviada por push ao pipeline do middleware do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1051">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1052">O pipeline do middleware manipula a solicitação e a passa como uma instância de `HttpContext` para a lógica do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1052">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1053">O middleware adicionado pela integração do IIS atualiza o esquema, o IP remoto e pathbase para encaminhar a solicitação para o Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1053">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1054">A resposta do aplicativo é retornada ao IIS, que a retorna por push para o cliente HTTP que iniciou a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1054">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1055">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configura o servidor [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) como o servidor Web e habilita a integração do IIS, configurando o caminho base e a porta para o [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1055">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configures [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server as the web server and enables IIS Integration by configuring the base path and port for the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1056">O Módulo do ASP.NET Core gera uma porta dinâmica a ser atribuída ao processo de back-end.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1056">The ASP.NET Core Module generates a dynamic port to assign to the backend process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1057">`CreateDefaultBuilder` chama o método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1057">`CreateDefaultBuilder` calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1058">`UseIISIntegration` configura o Kestrel para escutar na porta dinâmica no endereço IP do localhost (`127.0.0.1`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1058">`UseIISIntegration` configures Kestrel to listen on the dynamic port at the localhost IP address (`127.0.0.1`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1059">Se a porta dinâmica for 1234, o Kestrel escutará em `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1059">If the dynamic port is 1234, Kestrel listens at `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1060">Essa configuração substitui outras configurações de URL fornecidas por:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1060">This configuration replaces other URL configurations provided by:</span></span>

* `UseUrls`
* [<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1061">API de escuta do Kestrel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1061">Kestrel's Listen API</span></span>](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel#endpoint-configuration)
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1062">[Configuração](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (ou [opção --urls de linha de comando](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1062">[Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (or [command-line --urls option](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1063">As chamadas a `UseUrls` ou à API `Listen` do Kestrel não são necessárias ao usar o módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1063">Calls to `UseUrls` or Kestrel's `Listen` API aren't required when using the module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1064">Se `UseUrls` ou `Listen` for chamado, o Kestrel escutará na porta especificada somente durante a execução do aplicativo sem o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1064">If `UseUrls` or `Listen` is called, Kestrel listens on the port specified only when running the app without IIS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1065">Para orientação sobre a configuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1065">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1066">Para saber mais sobre hospedagem, confira [Host no ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1066">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1067">Configuração de aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1067">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1068">Habilitar os componentes de IISIntegration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1068">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1069">Ao criar um host no `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), chame <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> para habilitar a integração do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1069">When building a host in `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IWebHostBuilder CreateWebHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1070">Para obter mais informações sobre o `CreateDefaultBuilder`, consulte <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1070">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1071">Opções do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1071">IIS options</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1072">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1072">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1073">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1073">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1074">Setting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1074">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1075">Se `true`, o Servidor do IIS define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1075">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1076">Se `false`, o servidor fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1076">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1077">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1077">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1078">Para obter mais informações, veja [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1078">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1079">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1079">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1080">Para configurar opções do IIS, inclua uma configuração de serviço para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1080">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1081">O exemplo a seguir impede que o aplicativo preencha `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1081">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1082">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1082">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1083">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1083">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1084">Setting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1084">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1085">Se `true`, o [middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1085">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1086">Se `false`, o middleware fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1086">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1087">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1087">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1088">Saiba mais no tópico [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1088">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1089">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1089">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1090">Se `true` e o cabeçalho da solicitação `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` estiverem presentes, o `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` será populado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1090">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1091">Servidor proxy e cenários de balanceador de carga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1091">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>
