<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1092">O [Middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), que configura o Middleware de cabeçalhos encaminhados, e o módulo do ASP.NET Core, são configurados para encaminhar o esquema (HTTP/HTTPS) e o endereço IP remoto de onde a solicitação foi originada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1092">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), which configures Forwarded Headers Middleware, and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the scheme (HTTP/HTTPS) and the remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1093">Configuração adicional pode ser necessária para aplicativos hospedados atrás de servidores proxy adicionais e balanceadores de carga.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1093">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1094">Para obter mais informações, veja [Configurar o ASP.NET Core para trabalhar com servidores proxy e balanceadores de carga](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1094">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1095">Arquivo web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1095">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1096">O arquivo *web.config* configura o [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1096">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1097">Criando, transformar e publicar o arquivo *Web.config* é tratado por um destino do MSBuild (`_TransformWebConfig`) quando o projeto é publicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1097">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1098">Este destino está presente nos destinos do SDK da Web (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1098">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1099">O SDK é definido na parte superior do arquivo de projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1099">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1100">Se um arquivo *web.config* não estiver presente no projeto, ele será criado com o *processPath* e os *argumentos* corretos para configurar o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e será transferido para o [resultado publicado](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1100">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1101">Se um arquivo *web.config* estiver presente no projeto, ele será transformado com o *processPath* e os *argumentos* corretos para configurar o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e será movido para o resultado publicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1101">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1102">A transformação não altera as definições de configuração do IIS no arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1102">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1103">O arquivo *web.config* pode fornecer configurações adicionais do IIS que controlam módulos ativos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1103">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1104">Para saber mais sobre os módulos do IIS que podem processar solicitações com aplicativos do ASP.NET Core, veja o tópico [Módulos do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1104">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1105">Para impedir que o SDK da Web transforme o arquivo de *web.config* , use a **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** propriedade no arquivo de projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1105">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1106">Ao impedir que o SDK Web transforme o arquivo, o *processPath* e os *argumentos* devem ser definidos manualmente pelo desenvolvedor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1106">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1107">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1107">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1108">Local do arquivo web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1108">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1109">Para configurar o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) corretamente, o arquivo de *web.config* deve estar presente no caminho raiz do [conteúdo](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) (normalmente o caminho base do aplicativo) do aplicativo implantado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1109">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1110">Esse é o mesmo local que o caminho físico do site fornecido ao IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1110">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1111">O arquivo *web.config* é necessário na raiz do aplicativo para habilitar a publicação de vários aplicativos usando a Implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1111">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1112">Existem arquivos confidenciais no caminho físico do aplicativo, como \* \<assembly>.runtimeconfig.jsem*, \* \<assembly> . xml* (comentários de documentação XML) e \* \<assembly>.deps.jsem\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1112">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1113">Quando o arquivo *web.config* estiver presente e o site for iniciado normalmente, o IIS não atenderá a esses arquivos confidenciais se eles forem solicitados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1113">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1114">Se o arquivo *web.config* estiver ausente, nomeado incorretamente ou se não for possível configurar o site para inicialização normal, o IIS poderá servir arquivos confidenciais publicamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1114">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1115">**O arquivo de *web.config* deve estar presente na implantação o tempo todo, corretamente nomeado e ser capaz de configurar o site para inicialização normal. Nunca remova o arquivo de *web.config* de uma implantação de produção.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1115">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1116">Transformação do Web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1116">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1117">Se você precisar transformar o *Web.config* em publicação (por exemplo, definir variáveis ​​de ambiente com base na configuração, no perfil ou no ambiente), consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1117">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish (for example, set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment), see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1118">Configuração do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1118">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1119">**Sistemas operacionais do Windows Server**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1119">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1120">Habilite a função **Servidor Web (IIS)** e estabeleça serviços de função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1120">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1121">Use o assistente **Adicionar Funções e Recursos** por meio do menu **Gerenciar** ou do link no **Gerenciador do Servidor**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1121">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1122">Na etapa **Funções de Servidor**, marque a caixa de **Servidor Web (IIS)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1122">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![A função de Servidor Web IIS é selecionada na etapa Selecionar funções de servidor.](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1124">Após a etapa **Recursos**, a etapa **Serviços de função** é carregada para o servidor Web (IIS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1124">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1125">Selecione os serviços de função do IIS desejados ou aceite os serviços de função padrão fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1125">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![Os serviços de função padrão são selecionados na etapa Selecionar serviços de função.](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1127">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1127">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1128">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós: segurança do **servidor Web**  >  **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1128">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1129">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1129">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1130">Para obter mais informações, consulte [autenticação \<windowsAuthentication> do Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar a autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1130">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1131">**WebSockets (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1131">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1132">O WebSockets é compatível com o ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1132">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1133">Para habilitar WebSockets, expanda os seguintes nós: desenvolvimento de aplicativo de **servidor Web**  >  **Application Development**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1133">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1134">Selecione o recurso **Protocolo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1134">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1135">Para obter mais informações, consulte [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1135">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1136">Continue para a etapa **Confirmação** para instalar os serviços e a função de servidor Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1136">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1137">Uma reinicialização de servidor/IIS não é necessária após a instalação da função do **servidor Web (IIS)** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1137">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1138">**Sistemas operacionais de área de trabalho do Windows**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1138">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1139">Habilite o **Console de Gerenciamento do IIS** e os **Serviços na World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1139">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1140">Navegue até **Painel de Controle** > **Programas** > **Programas e Recursos** > **Ativar ou desativar recursos do Windows** (lado esquerdo da tela).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1140">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1141">Abra o nó **Serviços de Informações da Internet**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1141">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1142">Abra o nó **Ferramentas de Gerenciamento da Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1142">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1143">Marque a caixa de **Console de Gerenciamento do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1143">Check the box for **IIS Management Console**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1144">Marque a caixa de **Serviços na World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1144">Check the box for **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1145">Aceite os recursos padrão dos **Serviços na World Wide Web** ou personalize os recursos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1145">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1146">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1146">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1147">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós: segurança **dos serviços de World Wide Web**  >  **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1147">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1148">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1148">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1149">Para obter mais informações, consulte [autenticação \<windowsAuthentication> do Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar a autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1149">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1150">**WebSockets (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1150">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1151">O WebSockets é compatível com o ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1151">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1152">Para habilitar WebSockets, expanda os seguintes nós: recursos de desenvolvimento de aplicativos **World Wide Web Services**  >  **Application Development Features**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1152">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1153">Selecione o recurso **Protocolo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1153">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1154">Para obter mais informações, consulte [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1154">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1155">Se a instalação do IIS exigir uma reinicialização, reinicie o sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1155">If the IIS installation requires a restart, restart the system.</span></span>

![O Console de Gerenciamento do IIS e os Serviços na World Wide Web estão selecionados em Recursos do Windows.](index/_static/windows-features-win10.png)

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1157">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1157">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1158">Instale o *pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core* no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1158">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1159">O pacote instala o tempo de execução do .NET Core, a biblioteca do .NET Core e o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1159">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1160">O módulo permite que aplicativos do ASP.NET Core sejam executados por trás do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1160">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1161">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado antes do IIS, a instalação do pacote deverá ser reparada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1161">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1162">Execute o instalador do pacote de hospedagem novamente depois de instalar o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1162">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1163">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado após a instalação da versão de 64 bits (x64) do .NET Core, os SDKs poderão parecer estar ausentes ([Nenhum SDK do .NET Core foi detectado](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1163">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1164">Para resolver o problema, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1164">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="download"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1165">Baixar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1165">Download</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1166">Navegue até a página [baixar o .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1166">Navigate to the [Download .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1167">Selecione a versão do .NET Core desejada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1167">Select the desired .NET Core version.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1168">Na coluna **Executar aplicativos – runtime**, localize a linha da versão de runtime do .NET Core desejada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1168">In the **Run apps - Runtime** column, find the row of the .NET Core runtime version desired.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1169">Baixe o instalador usando o link **pacote de hospedagem** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1169">Download the installer using the **Hosting Bundle** link.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1170">Alguns instaladores contêm versões de lançamento que atingiram o EOL (fim da vida útil) e não têm mais suporte da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1170">Some installers contain release versions that have reached their end of life (EOL) and are no longer supported by Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1171">Para saber mais, confira a [política de suporte](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1171">For more information, see the [support policy](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1172">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1172">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1173">Execute o instalador no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1173">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1174">Os parâmetros a seguir estão disponíveis ao executar o instalador por meio de um shell de comando do administrador:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1174">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1175">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Ignorar a instalação do módulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1175">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1176">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Ignorar a instalação do tempo de execução do .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1176">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1177">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1177">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1178">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Ignorar a instalação da estrutura compartilhada ASP.NET (ASP.NET Runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1178">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1179">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1179">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1180">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Ignorar a instalação de tempos de execução x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1180">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1181">Use esse parâmetro quando você souber que não hospedará aplicativos de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1181">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1182">Se houver uma possibilidade de hospedar aplicativos de 32 bits e 64 bits no futuro, não use esse parâmetro e instale ambos os runtimes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1182">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1183">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Desabilite a verificação para usar uma configuração compartilhada do IIS quando a configuração compartilhada (*applicationHost.config*) estiver no mesmo computador que a instalação do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1183">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (*applicationHost.config*) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1184">*Disponível somente para instaladores do ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou Hosting Bundler posterior.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1184">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1185">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1185">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1186">Reinicie o sistema ou execute os seguintes comandos em um shell de comando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1186">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1187">A reinicialização do IIS identifica uma alteração no CAMINHO do sistema, que é uma variável de ambiente, realizada pelo instalador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1187">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1188">Não é necessário interromper manualmente os sites individuais no IIS ao instalar o pacote de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1188">It isn't necessary to manually stop individual sites in IIS when installing the Hosting Bundle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1189">Aplicativos hospedados (sites do IIS) são reiniciados quando o IIS é reiniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1189">Hosted apps (IIS sites) restart when IIS restarts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1190">Os aplicativos são iniciados novamente quando recebem sua primeira solicitação, incluindo a partir do [módulo de inicialização do aplicativo](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1190">Apps start up again when they receive their first request, including from the [Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1191">ASP.NET Core adota o comportamento de roll-forward para versões de patch de pacotes de estrutura compartilhados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1191">ASP.NET Core adopts roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1192">Quando os aplicativos hospedados pelo IIS são reiniciados com o IIS, os aplicativos são carregados com as versões de patch mais recentes de seus pacotes referenciados quando recebem sua primeira solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1192">When apps hosted by IIS restart with IIS, the apps load with the latest patch releases of their referenced packages when they receive their first request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1193">Se o IIS não for reiniciado, os aplicativos serão reiniciados e exibirão o comportamento de roll-forward quando seus processos de trabalho forem reciclados e receberem sua primeira solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1193">If IIS isn't restarted, apps restart and exhibit roll-forward behavior when their worker processes are recycled and they receive their first request.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1194">Para obter informações sobre a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS, consulte [Módulo do ASP.NET Core com a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1194">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1195">Instalar a Implantação da Web durante a publicação com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1195">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1196">Ao implantar aplicativos para servidores com [Implantação da Web](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), instale a versão mais recente da Implantação da Web no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1196">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1197">Para instalar a Implantação da Web, use o [WebPI (Web Platform Installer)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) ou obtenha um instalador diretamente no [Centro de Download da Microsoft](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1197">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1198">O método preferencial é usar o WebPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1198">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1199">O WebPI oferece uma instalação autônoma e uma configuração para provedores de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1199">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1200">Criar o site do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1200">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1201">No sistema de hospedagem, crie uma pasta para conter arquivos e pastas publicados do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1201">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1202">Em uma etapa a seguir, o caminho da pasta é fornecido ao IIS como o caminho físico para o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1202">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1203">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de arquivo e a pasta de implantação de um aplicativo, confira <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1203">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1204">No Gerenciador do IIS, abra o nó do servidor no painel **conexões** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1204">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1205">Clique com botão direito do mouse na pasta **Sites**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1205">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1206">Selecione **Adicionar Site** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1206">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1207">Forneça um **Nome do site** e defina o **Caminho físico** como a pasta de implantação do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1207">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1208">Forneça a configuração de **Associação** e crie o site selecionando **OK**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1208">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![Forneça o Nome do site, o caminho físico e o Nome do host na etapa Adicionar Site.](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1210">Associações de curinga de nível superior (`http://*:80/` e `http://+:80`) **não** devem ser usadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1210">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1211">Associações de curinga de nível superior podem abrir o aplicativo para vulnerabilidades de segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1211">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1212">Isso se aplica a curingas fortes e fracos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1212">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1213">Use nomes de host explícitos em vez de curingas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1213">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1214">Associações de curinga de subdomínio (por exemplo, `*.mysub.com`) não têm esse risco de segurança se você controlar o domínio pai completo (em vez de `*.com`, o qual é vulnerável).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1214">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1215">Veja [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1215">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1216">No nó do servidor, selecione **Pools de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1216">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1217">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do site e selecione **Configurações Básicas** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1217">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1218">Na janela **Editar Pool de Aplicativos**, defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1218">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![Defina Sem Código Gerenciado para a versão do CLR do .NET.](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1220">O ASP.NET Core é executado em um processo separado e gerencia o runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1220">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1221">O ASP.NET Core não depende do carregamento do CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET)&mdash;o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) para o .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1221">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1222">Definir a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** é opcional, porém recomendado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1222">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1223">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior*: para uma [implantação autocontida](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) de 64 bits (x64) que usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](#in-process-hosting-model), desabilite o pool de aplicativos para processos de 32 bits (x86).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1223">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*: For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1224">Na barra lateral **Ações** do Gerenciador do IIS > **Pools de Aplicativos**, selecione **Definir Padrões do Pool de Aplicativos** ou **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1224">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools**, select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1225">Localize **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits** e defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1225">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1226">Essa configuração não afeta os aplicativos implantados para a [hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1226">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1227">Confirme se a identidade do modelo de processo tem as permissões apropriadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1227">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1228">Se a identidade padrão do pool de aplicativos (**modelo de processo**  >  **Identity** ) for alterada **de Identity ApplicationPool** para outra identidade, verifique se a nova identidade tem as permissões necessárias para acessar a pasta, o banco de dados e outros recursos necessários do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1228">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1229">Por exemplo, o pool de aplicativos requer acesso de leitura e gravação às pastas nas quais o aplicativo lê e grava os arquivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1229">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1230">**Configuração de Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1230">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1231">Para saber mais, veja [Configurar a Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1231">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1232">Implantar o aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1232">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1233">Implante o aplicativo na pasta **caminho físico** do IIS que foi estabelecida na seção [Criar o site do IIS](#create-the-iis-site).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1233">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1234">[Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) é o mecanismo recomendado para implantação, mas existem várias opções para mover o aplicativo da pasta *publicar* do projeto para a pasta de implantação do sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1234">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1235">Implantação da Web com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1235">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1236">Consulte o tópico [Perfis de publicação do Visual Studio para implantação de aplicativos ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) para saber como criar um perfil de publicação para uso com a Implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1236">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1237">Se o provedor de hospedagem fornecer um Perfil de Publicação ou o suporte para a criação de um, baixe o perfil e importe-o usando a caixa de diálogo **Publicar** do Visual Studio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1237">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

![Página de caixa de diálogo Publicar](index/_static/pub-dialog.png)

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1239">Implantação da Web fora do Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1239">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1240">Também é possível usar a [Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) fora do Visual Studio na linha de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1240">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1241">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Ferramenta de Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1241">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1242">Alternativas à Implantação da Web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1242">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1243">Use qualquer um dos vários métodos para mover o aplicativo para o sistema host, como cópia manual, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) ou [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1243">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1244">Para obter mais informações sobre a implantação do ASP.NET Core no IIS, consulte a seção [Recursos de implantação para administradores do IIS](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1244">For more information on ASP.NET Core deployment to IIS, see the [Deployment resources for IIS administrators](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators) section.</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1245">Procurar no site</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1245">Browse the website</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1246">Depois de implantar o aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem, faça uma solicitação para um dos pontos de extremidade públicos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1246">After the app is deployed to the hosting system, make a request to one of the app's public endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1247">No exemplo a seguir, o site está associado a um **Nome do Host** IIS de `www.mysite.com` na **Porta** `80`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1247">In the following example, the site is bound to an IIS **Host name** of `www.mysite.com` on **Port** `80`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1248">É feita uma solicitação para `http://www.mysite.com`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1248">A request is made to `http://www.mysite.com`:</span></span>

![O navegador Microsoft Edge carregou a página de inicialização do IIS.](index/_static/browsewebsite.png)

## <a name="locked-deployment-files"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1250">Arquivos de implantação bloqueados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1250">Locked deployment files</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1251">Os arquivos na pasta de implantação são bloqueados quando o aplicativo está em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1251">Files in the deployment folder are locked when the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1252">Os arquivos bloqueados não podem ser substituídos durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1252">Locked files can't be overwritten during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1253">Para liberar os arquivos bloqueados em uma implantação, interrompa o pool de aplicativos usando **uma** das abordagens a seguir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1253">To release locked files in a deployment, stop the app pool using **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1254">Use a Implantação da Web e referencie `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` no arquivo do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1254">Use Web Deploy and reference `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` in the project file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1255">Um arquivo *app_offline.htm* é colocado na raiz do diretório de aplicativo da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1255">An *app_offline.htm* file is placed at the root of the web app directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1256">Quando o arquivo estiver presente, o módulo do ASP.NET Core apenas desligará o aplicativo e servirá o arquivo *app_offline.htm* durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1256">When the file is present, the ASP.NET Core Module gracefully shuts down the app and serves the *app_offline.htm* file during the deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1257">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Referência de configuração do módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1257">For more information, see the [ASP.NET Core Module configuration reference](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1258">Manualmente interrompa o pool de aplicativos no Gerenciador do IIS no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1258">Manually stop the app pool in the IIS Manager on the server.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1259">Use o PowerShell para descartar *app_offline.htm* (requer o PowerShell 5 ou posterior):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1259">Use PowerShell to drop *app_offline.htm* (requires PowerShell 5 or later):</span></span>

  ```powershell
  $pathToApp = 'PATH_TO_APP'

  # Stop the AppPool
  New-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  # Provide script commands here to deploy the app

  # Restart the AppPool
  Remove-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  ```

## <a name="data-protection"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1260">Proteção de dados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1260">Data protection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1261">A [pilha Proteção de Dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) é usada por vários [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) ASP.NET Core, incluindo aqueles usados na autenticação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1261">The [ASP.NET Core Data Protection stack](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) is used by several ASP.NET Core [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index), including middleware used in authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1262">Mesmo se as APIs de proteção de dados não forem chamadas pelo código do usuário, a proteção de dados deverá ser configurada com um script de implantação ou no código do usuário para criar um [repositório de chaves](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management) criptográfico persistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1262">Even if Data Protection APIs aren't called by user code, data protection should be configured with a deployment script or in user code to create a persistent cryptographic [key store](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1263">Se a proteção de dados não estiver configurada, as chaves serão mantidas na memória e descartadas quando o aplicativo for reiniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1263">If data protection isn't configured, the keys are held in memory and discarded when the app restarts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1264">Se o token de autenticação for armazenado na memória quando o aplicativo for reiniciado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1264">If the key ring is stored in memory when the app restarts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1265">Os cookie tokens de autenticação baseados em todos os são invalidados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1265">All cookie-based authentication tokens are invalidated.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1266">Os usuários precisam entrar novamente na próxima solicitação deles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1266">Users are required to sign in again on their next request.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1267">Todos os dados protegidos com o token de autenticação não poderão mais ser descriptografados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1267">Any data protected with the key ring can no longer be decrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1268">Isso pode incluir [tokens CSRF](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) e [ASP.NET Core cookie s de TempData do MVC](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1268">This may include [CSRF tokens](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) and [ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookies](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1269">Para configurar a proteção de dados no IIS para persistir o token de autenticação, use **uma** das seguintes abordagens:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1269">To configure data protection under IIS to persist the key ring, use **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1270">**Criar chaves de registro de proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1270">**Create Data Protection Registry Keys**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1271">As chaves de proteção de dados usadas pelos aplicativos ASP.NET Core são armazenadas no registro externo aos aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1271">Data protection keys used by ASP.NET Core apps are stored in the registry external to the apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1272">Para persistir as chaves de determinado aplicativo, crie uma chave de registro para o pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1272">To persist the keys for a given app, create registry keys for the app pool.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1273">Para instalações autônomas do IIS não Web Farm, você pode usar o [script Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 de Proteção de Dados do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) para cada pool de aplicativos usado com um aplicativo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1273">For standalone, non-webfarm IIS installations, the [Data Protection Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) can be used for each app pool used with an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1274">Esse script cria uma chave de registro no registro HKLM que é acessível apenas para a conta do processo de trabalho do pool de aplicativos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1274">This script creates a registry key in the HKLM registry that's accessible only to the worker process account of the app's app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1275">As chaves são criptografadas em repouso usando a DPAPI com uma chave para todo o computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1275">Keys are encrypted at rest using DPAPI with a machine-wide key.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1276">Em cenários de web farm, um aplicativo pode ser configurado para usar um caminho UNC para armazenar seu token de autenticação de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1276">In web farm scenarios, an app can be configured to use a UNC path to store its data protection key ring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1277">Por padrão, as chaves de proteção de dados não são criptografadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1277">By default, the data protection keys aren't encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1278">Garanta que as permissões de arquivo de o compartilhamento de rede sejam limitadas à conta do Windows na qual o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1278">Ensure that the file permissions for the network share are limited to the Windows account the app runs under.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1279">Um certificado X509 pode ser usado para proteger chaves em repouso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1279">An X509 certificate can be used to protect keys at rest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1280">Considere um mecanismo para permitir aos usuários carregar certificados: coloque os certificados no repositório de certificados confiáveis do usuário e certifique-se de que eles estejam disponíveis em todos os computadores nos quais o aplicativo do usuário é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1280">Consider a mechanism to allow users to upload certificates: Place certificates into the user's trusted certificate store and ensure they're available on all machines where the user's app runs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1281">Veja [Configurar a proteção de dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) para obter detalhes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1281">See [Configure ASP.NET Core Data Protection](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) for details.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1282">**Configurar o pool de aplicativos do IIS para carregar o perfil do usuário**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1282">**Configure the IIS Application Pool to load the user profile**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1283">Essa configuração está na seção **Modelo de processo** nas **Configurações avançadas** do pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1283">This setting is in the **Process Model** section under the **Advanced Settings** for the app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1284">Defina **carregar perfil do usuário** como `True` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1284">Set **Load User Profile** to `True`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1285">Quando definido como `True`, as chaves são armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário e protegidas usando DPAPI com uma chave específica para a conta de usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1285">When set to `True`, keys are stored in the user profile directory and protected using DPAPI with a key specific to the user account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1286">As chaves são persistidas para a pasta *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1286">Keys are persisted to the *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys* folder.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1287">O [atributo setProfileEnvironment](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) do pool de aplicativos também deve ser habilitado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1287">The app pool's [setProfileEnvironment attribute](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) must also be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1288">O valor padrão de `setProfileEnvironment` é `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1288">The default value of `setProfileEnvironment` is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1289">Em alguns cenários (por exemplo, um SO Windows), `setProfileEnvironment` é definido como `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1289">In some scenarios (for example, Windows OS), `setProfileEnvironment` is set to `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1290">Se as chaves não estiverem armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário como esperado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1290">If keys aren't stored in the user profile directory as expected:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1291">navegue até a pasta *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1291">Navigate to the *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config* folder.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1292">Abra o arquivo *applicationHost.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1292">Open the *applicationHost.config* file.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1293">Localize o elemento `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1293">Locate the `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` element.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1294">Confirme se o atributo `setProfileEnvironment` não está presente, que tem como padrão o valor `true`, ou defina explicitamente o valor do atributo como `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1294">Confirm that the `setProfileEnvironment` attribute isn't present, which defaults the value to `true`, or explicitly set the attribute's value to `true`.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1295">**Usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1295">**Use the file system as a key ring store**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1296">Ajuste o código do aplicativo para [usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1296">Adjust the app code to [use the file system as a key ring store](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1297">Use um certificado X509 para proteger o token de autenticação e verifique se ele é um certificado confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1297">Use an X509 certificate to protect the key ring and ensure the certificate is a trusted certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1298">Se o certificado for autoassinado, você deverá colocá-lo no repositório Raiz confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1298">If the certificate is self-signed, place the certificate in the Trusted Root store.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1299">Ao usar o IIS em uma web farm:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1299">When using IIS in a web farm:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1300">Use um compartilhamento de arquivos que pode ser acessado por todos os computadores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1300">Use a file share that all machines can access.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1301">Implante um certificado X509 em cada computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1301">Deploy an X509 certificate to each machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1302">Configure a [proteção de dados no código](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1302">Configure [data protection in code](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1303">**Definir uma política para todo o computador para proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1303">**Set a machine-wide policy for data protection**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1304">O sistema de proteção de dados tem suporte limitado para a configuração da [política de todo o computador](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) padrão para todos os aplicativos que consomem as APIs de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1304">The data protection system has limited support for setting a default [machine-wide policy](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) for all apps that consume the Data Protection APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1305">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1305">For more information, see <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span></span>

## <a name="virtual-directories"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1306">Diretórios virtuais</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1306">Virtual Directories</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1307">[Diretórios virtuais IIS](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) não são compatíveis com aplicativos ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1307">[IIS Virtual Directories](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) aren't supported with ASP.NET Core apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1308">Um aplicativo pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo](#sub-applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1308">An app can be hosted as a [sub-application](#sub-applications).</span></span>

## <a name="sub-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1309">Subaplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1309">Sub-applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1310">Um aplicativo ASP.NET Core pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo IIS (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1310">An ASP.NET Core app can be hosted as an [IIS sub-application (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1311">A parte do caminho do subaplicativo se torna parte da URL raiz do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1311">The sub-app's path becomes part of the root app's URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1312">Um subaplicativo não deve incluir o módulo do ASP.NET Core como um manipulador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1312">A sub-app shouldn't include the ASP.NET Core Module as a handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1313">Se o módulo for adicionado como um manipulador em um arquivo de *web.config* de subaplicativo, um *erro de servidor interno 500,19* referenciando o arquivo de configuração com falha será recebido ao tentar procurar o subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1313">If the module is added as a handler in a sub-app's *web.config* file, a *500.19 Internal Server Error* referencing the faulty config file is received when attempting to browse the sub-app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1314">O seguinte exemplo mostra um arquivo *web.config* publicado de um subaplicativo ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1314">The following example shows a published *web.config* file for an ASP.NET Core sub-app:</span></span>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<configuration>
  <system.webServer>
    <aspNetCore processPath="dotnet" 
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll" 
      stdoutLogEnabled="false" 
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout" />
  </system.webServer>
</configuration>
```

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1315">Ao hospedar um subaplicativo não ASP.NET Core abaixo de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, remova explicitamente o manipulador herdado no arquivo *web.config* do subaplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1315">When hosting a non-ASP.NET Core sub-app underneath an ASP.NET Core app, explicitly remove the inherited handler in the sub-app's *web.config* file:</span></span>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<configuration>
  <system.webServer>
    <handlers>
      <remove name="aspNetCore" />
    </handlers>
    <aspNetCore processPath="dotnet" 
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll" 
      stdoutLogEnabled="false" 
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout" />
  </system.webServer>
</configuration>
```

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1316">Links de ativos estáticos dentro do subaplicativo devem usar a notação de sinal de til e barra (`~/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1316">Static asset links within the sub-app should use tilde-slash (`~/`) notation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1317">A notação de sinal de til e barra aciona um [Auxiliar de Marca](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) para preceder a base de caminho do subaplicativo ao link relativo renderizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1317">Tilde-slash notation triggers a [Tag Helper](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) to prepend the sub-app's pathbase to the rendered relative link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1318">Para um subaplicativo no `/subapp_path`, uma imagem vinculada com `src="~/image.png"` é renderizada como `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1318">For a sub-app at `/subapp_path`, an image linked with `src="~/image.png"` is rendered as `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1319">O Middleware de Arquivo Estático do aplicativo raiz não processa a solicitação de arquivo estático.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1319">The root app's Static File Middleware doesn't process the static file request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1320">A solicitação é processada pelo Middleware de Arquivo Estático do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1320">The request is processed by the sub-app's Static File Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1321">Se um atributo de ativo estático `src` for definido como um caminho absoluto (por exemplo, `src="/image.png"`), o link será renderizado sem a base de caminho do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1321">If a static asset's `src` attribute is set to an absolute path (for example, `src="/image.png"`), the link is rendered without the sub-app's pathbase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1322">O Middleware de Arquivos Estáticos do aplicativo raiz tenta fornecer o ativo do [webroot](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root) da raiz do aplicativo, que resulta em uma resposta *404 – Não encontrado*, a menos que o ativo estático esteja disponível no aplicativo raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1322">The root app's Static File Middleware attempts to serve the asset from the root app's [web root](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root), which results in a *404 - Not Found* response unless the static asset is available from the root app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1323">Para hospedar um aplicativo ASP.NET Core como um subaplicativo em outro aplicativo do ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1323">To host an ASP.NET Core app as a sub-app under another ASP.NET Core app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1324">Estabeleça um pool de aplicativos para o subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1324">Establish an app pool for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1325">Defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** porque o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) do .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho, não no CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1325">Set the **.NET CLR Version** to **No Managed Code** because the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process, not the desktop CLR (.NET CLR).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1326">Adicione o site raiz no Gerenciador do IIS com o subaplicativo em uma pasta no site raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1326">Add the root site in IIS Manager with the sub-app in a folder under the root site.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1327">Clique com o botão direito do mouse na pasta do subaplicativo no Gerenciador do IIS e selecione **Converter em aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1327">Right-click the sub-app folder in IIS Manager and select **Convert to Application**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1328">Na caixa de diálogo **Adicionar Aplicativo**, use o botão **Selecionar** no **Pool de Aplicativos** para atribuir o pool de aplicativos que você criou ao subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1328">In the **Add Application** dialog, use the **Select** button for the **Application Pool** to assign the app pool that you created for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1329">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1329">Select **OK**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1330">A atribuição de um pool de aplicativos separado para o subaplicativo é um requisito ao usar o modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1330">The assignment of a separate app pool to the sub-app is a requirement when using the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1331">Para obter mais informações sobre o modelo de hospedagem em processo e como configurar o módulo ASP.NET Core, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1331">For more information on the in-process hosting model and configuring the ASP.NET Core Module, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-of-iis-with-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1332">Configuração do IIS com web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1332">Configuration of IIS with web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1333">A configuração do IIS é influenciada pela seção `<system.webServer>` do *web.config* para cenários do IIS que são funcionais para aplicativos ASP.NET Core com o Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1333">IIS configuration is influenced by the `<system.webServer>` section of *web.config* for IIS scenarios that are functional for ASP.NET Core apps with the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1334">Por exemplo, a configuração do IIS é funcional para a compactação dinâmica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1334">For example, IIS configuration is functional for dynamic compression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1335">Se o IIS for configurado no nível do servidor para usar a compactação dinâmica, o elemento `<urlCompression>` no arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo pode desabilitá-la para um aplicativo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1335">If IIS is configured at the server level to use dynamic compression, the `<urlCompression>` element in the app's *web.config* file can disable it for an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1336">Para obter mais informações, consulte estes tópicos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1336">For more information, see the following topics:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="54f8a-1337">Referência de configuração para\<system.webServer></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54f8a-1337">Configuration reference for \<system.webServer></span></span>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/)
* <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>
* <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules>
